REVENUE METRICS

SQL & TABLEAU

Project Overview

This project focuses on analyzing revenue metrics using SQL and Tableau, providing insights into user subscriptions and financial performance.

Business Question

How do our recurring revenue and paying user base evolve over time and what drives these changes?

Dataset

  • Source: PostgreSQL database
  • Structure: Payment data including user_id, payment_date, revenue_amount_usd, plus user-level attributes (language, age, game and device type)

Outcome

A two-page Tableau dashboard allowing product and growth managers to:

  • Monitor revenue dynamics (MRR, ARPPU, LTV)
  • Analyze user movement patterns (churn, reactivation, cohort retention)
  • Identify drivers of revenue change and user base growth/decline

SQL Logic

ETL Strategy

  • CTEs to construct base dataset with all payment events
  • Monthly aggregation using DATE_TRUNC('month', payment_date)
  • Joins and LAG()/LEAD() functions to detect churn, reactivation, and expansion/contraction
  • Output stored as clean, analysis-ready table
Click to View SQL Query 
                WITH base AS (
                  SELECT 
                    user_id,
                    payment_date,
                    revenue_amount_usd,
                    DATE_TRUNC('month', payment_date::DATE)::DATE AS paid_month,
                    game_name,
                    language,
                    age,
                    has_older_device_model,
                    LAG(DATE_TRUNC('month', payment_date::DATE)::DATE) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id ORDER BY payment_date) AS previous_paid_month,
                    LEAD(DATE_TRUNC('month', payment_date::DATE)::DATE) OVER (PARTITION BY user_id ORDER BY payment_date) AS next_paid_month
                  FROM newtable_oh
                ),

                dataset_end AS (
                  SELECT MAX(DATE_TRUNC('month', payment_date::DATE))::DATE AS max_month
                  FROM newtable_oh
                ),

                monthly_revenue AS (
                  SELECT 
                    user_id,
                    DATE_TRUNC('month', payment_date::DATE)::DATE AS paid_month,
                    SUM(revenue_amount_usd) AS total_month_revenue
                  FROM newtable_oh
                  GROUP BY user_id, paid_month
                )

                SELECT 
                  b.user_id,
                  b.payment_date,
                  b.revenue_amount_usd,
                  b.paid_month,
                  b.previous_paid_month,
                  b.next_paid_month,
                  CASE 
                    WHEN b.next_paid_month IS NULL AND b.paid_month + INTERVAL '1 month' <= de.max_month
                    THEN (b.paid_month + INTERVAL '1 month')::DATE
                    WHEN b.next_paid_month IS NOT NULL AND b.next_paid_month != b.paid_month + INTERVAL '1 month'
                    THEN (b.paid_month + INTERVAL '1 month')::DATE
                  END AS churn_month,
                  mr.total_month_revenue AS current_month_revenue,

                  -- Reactivated user flag and revenue
                  CASE 
                    WHEN b.previous_paid_month IS NOT NULL AND b.previous_paid_month != b.paid_month - INTERVAL '1 month' THEN 1 
                    ELSE 0
                  END AS reactivated_users,
                  CASE 
                    WHEN b.previous_paid_month IS NOT NULL AND b.previous_paid_month != b.paid_month - INTERVAL '1 month' 
                    THEN b.revenue_amount_usd 
                    ELSE 0 
                  END AS reactivated_mrr,

                  -- Expansion and Contraction revenue
                  CASE 
                    WHEN b.previous_paid_month = b.paid_month - INTERVAL '1 month'
                    AND mr.total_month_revenue > 
                            (SELECT total_month_revenue
                            FROM monthly_revenue
                            WHERE user_id = b.user_id 
                            AND paid_month = b.previous_paid_month)
                    THEN mr.total_month_revenue - 
                        (SELECT total_month_revenue
                          FROM monthly_revenue
                          WHERE user_id = b.user_id 
                          AND paid_month = b.previous_paid_month)
                    ELSE 0
                  END AS expansion_revenue,

                  CASE 
                    WHEN b.previous_paid_month = b.paid_month - INTERVAL '1 month'
                    AND mr.total_month_revenue < 
                            (SELECT total_month_revenue
                            FROM monthly_revenue
                            WHERE user_id = b.user_id 
                            AND paid_month = b.previous_paid_month)
                    THEN (SELECT total_month_revenue
                          FROM monthly_revenue
                          WHERE user_id = b.user_id 
                          AND paid_month = b.previous_paid_month) - mr.total_month_revenue
                    ELSE 0
                  END AS contraction_revenue,

                  b.game_name,
                  b.language,
                  b.age,
                  b.has_older_device_model

                FROM base b
                LEFT JOIN monthly_revenue mr 
                  ON b.user_id = mr.user_id AND b.paid_month = mr.paid_month
                JOIN dataset_end de ON TRUE

                ORDER BY 2,1;

Tableau Dashboard

Key Insights

  • MRR is steadily increasing until October, driven largely by new paid users and expansion from existing ones
  • Churn spikes seen in last months — aligns with product changes or pricing experiments
  • ARPPU stabilizes despite user base growth — shows retention efforts are paying off
  • Top cohorts by LTV are users acquired in March and May — months with successful onboarding campaigns
  • Average user lifetime hovers around 3 months
